 khabaron ke mutabik film ke diarector shailendra singh ko ranvir ke manager ne phone par film na karne kii jaankaree di

 unhen film kii story bhi pasand ai thi

 shailendra unhen script bhejne hi vaale the
 Shailendra told nothing more than this

 wo us kirdaar main jaan foonkane ke liye puri mehnat or lagan se kaam karte hai
 Former Chief Minister of Jammu and Kashmir and People's Democratic Party (PDP) leader Mufti Mohammad Sayeed has said that instead of debate on the issue of war and war with Pakistan, there should be a national debate on peace restoration in Kashmir
